***место.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>место</a> (106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*město</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mésto</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>мест</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>place
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глухой.html>глухо́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">gluxóje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">backwoods</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:задеть.html>заде́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́е</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zadétʹ bolʹnóje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">cut to the quick</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:знать.html>знать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:свое.html>своё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">znatʹ svojó <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to know one’s place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:иметь.html>име́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">imétʹ <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">to take place, to happen; to exist</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:меняться.html>меня́ться</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́ми</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">menjátʹsja <b>mestámi</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">switch places</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ваш.html>ва́шем</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na vášem <b>méste</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">if I were you</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́х</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">na <b>mestáx</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">at the local level; in the provinces</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:общий.html>о́бщее</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">óbščeje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">banality, platitude</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">отхо́жее <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">otxóžeje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">outhouse</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:посадочный.html>поса́дочное</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">posádočnoje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">seat, seating place</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">прису́тственное <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prisútstvennoje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">public office (in the Russian Empire)</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:слабый.html>сла́бое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">sláboje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">weak spot</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:теплый.html>тёплое</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">tjóploje <b>mésto</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">gravy train, soft job</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>(<span class="gender"><abbr title="plural number">pl</abbr></span>) region, area
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вы</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бывать.html>быва́ли</a> когда́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́тих</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́х</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vy byváli kogdá-libo v étix <b>mestáx</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Have you ever been in these parts?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>site, scene
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сто</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:битва.html>би́твы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mésto</b> bítvy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">battle site</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>job, position
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:это.html>э́том</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>ме́сте</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:проработать.html>прорабо́тал</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:двадцать.html>два́дцать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:год.html>лет</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja na étom <b>méste</b> prorabótal dvádcatʹ let.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve been at this job for twenty years.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>piece (<i>of luggage</i>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сколько.html>ско́лько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>Вас</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>мест</a></b>?</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Skólʹko u Vas <b>mest</b>?</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">How many pieces of luggage do you have?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>room, space
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>На</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>оди́н</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сувенир.html>сувени́р</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:чемодан.html>чемода́не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:просто.html>про́сто</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:хватить.html>хвати́ло</a> <strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a></strong>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Na ješčó odín suvenír v čemodáne prósto ne xvatílo mesta.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">There was simply no room for another souvenir in the suitcase.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>месяц</a> (304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*měsęcь</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*mḗh₁n̥s</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mésjac</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяца</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяцы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяцев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>month
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">v <b>mésjac</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">per month</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>moon
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:молодой.html>молодо́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">molodój <b>mésjac</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">new moon</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">used in the expression</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:медовый.html>медо́вый</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">medóvyj <b>mésjac</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">honeymoon</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месяц.html>ме́сяц</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">mésjac</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:месячный.html>ме́сячный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">mésjačnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>monthly</li>
<li>month-long</li>
<li>month-old</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> moon

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> moonlit
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:месячный.html>ме́сячная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ночь.html>ночь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>mésjačnaja</b> nočʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>moonlit</b> night</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***металл.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:металл.html>мета́лл</a> (2958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">metallum</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металл.html>мета́лл</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metáll</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металл.html>мета́лла</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металл.html>мета́ллы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металл.html>мета́ллов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>metal (atomic element<b> or </b>material made of such atoms)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> metal (music style)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:металлист.html>металли́ст</a> (29105)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металлист.html>металли́ст</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metallíst</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металлист.html>металли́ста</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металлист.html>металли́сты</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:металлист.html>металли́стов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>metalworker</li>
<li>specialist in metals or metallurgy</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> musician who plays metal; member of a metal band</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">music</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> metalhead, headbanger</li></ol>

***метаморфоза.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метаморфоза.html>метаморфо́за</a> (23892)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метаморфоза.html>метаморфо́за</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metamorfóza</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метаморфоза.html>метаморфо́зы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метаморфоза.html>метаморфо́зы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метаморфоза.html>метаморфо́з</a></b>)

***метать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a> (9814)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">метати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*metàti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*met-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуть.html>метну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to throw, to cast, to toss
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:воин.html>во́ины</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>ме́чут</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:тяжелый.html>тяжёлые</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:копье.html>ко́пья</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Vóiny <b>méčut</b> tjažólyje kópʹja.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">The warriors are throwing heavy spears.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to spawn (roe)</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<div class="derivedterms" style="column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;;">
<p><i>imperfective</i>
</p>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">метати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*metàti</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to throw</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*met-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сметать.html>смета́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to baste, to tack
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:петля.html>пе́тли</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>metátʹ</b> pétli</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to make buttonholes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метаться.html>мета́ться</a> (4153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метаться.html>мета́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метнуться.html>метну́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to rush about</li>
<li>to toss, to toss about</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метать.html>мета́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">metátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метель.html>мете́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">metélʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метель.html>мете́ли</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метель.html>мете́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метель.html>мете́лей</a></b>)

***метить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a> (15748)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*mĕtiti</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Balto-Slavic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Balto-Slavic language">Proto-Balto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-bsl-pro">*mḗˀdīˀtei</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">med-éye-ti</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*med-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:метить.html>ме́тить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">métitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:пометить.html>поме́тить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to mark, to label</li>
<li>to aim</li>
<li>to drive at, to mean</li>
<li>to aspire <i>(to a position)</i></li></ol>

</ol>
